    { 1100525002;;DataItem;                  ;

                               Job.SETRANGE("Cumulation Filter", 0D, Job.GETRANGEMAX("Period Filter"));

                               Job.DPA_SetFilters(CurrReport.OBJECTID(FALSE));
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  BuildCostControl;

                                  DeterminePrognosisDate.DetermineBothDates(Job);

                                  PrevPrognosisFilter := GETRANGEMAX(PrevPrognosisFilter);

                                  PrevProgressFilter := GETRANGEMAX(PrevProgressFilter);

    { 1100525006;1;DataItem;CopyLoop         ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 ORDER(Ascending)
                                 WHERE(Number=FILTER(1|2));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF (NOT PrintSummary AND NOT PrintDetails) THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  CASE TRUE OF
                                    (PrintSummary AND PrintDetails):
                                      IF NOT (Number IN [1,2]) THEN
                                        CurrReport.SKIP;
                                    (PrintSummary AND NOT PrintDetails):
                                      IF Number = 2 THEN
                                        CurrReport.SKIP;
                                    (NOT PrintSummary AND PrintDetails):
                                      IF Number = 1 THEN
                                        CurrReport.SKIP;
                                  END;
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525063;2;Column;Number_CopyLoop    ;
               SourceExpr=Number }

    { 1100525007;2;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012047;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Project No.,Cost Type,Cost Object)
                                 ORDER(Ascending);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF (NOT PrintDetails) AND (CopyLoop.Number = 2) THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  Job.COPYFILTER("Period Filter", "Control Project/Cost Object"."Period Filter");
                                  Job.COPYFILTER("Cumulation Filter", "Control Project/Cost Object"."Cumulation Filter");
                                  Job.COPYFILTER("Prognosis Filter", "Control Project/Cost Object"."Prognosis Filter");
                                  Job.COPYFILTER("Progress Filter", "Control Project/Cost Object"."Progress Filter");
                                  SETRANGE("Purchase Action Filter");

                                  CostControlManagement.CalcFieldsCostObj("Control Project/Cost Object");
                                  TotalBudgetDec := Budget;
                                  ActualCostDec := "Actual Costs";
                                  PurchBudgetDec := "Purchase Budget";
                                  PrognosisDec := Prognosis;

                                  BudgetNotOnPurchaseActionDec := TotalBudgetDec - PurchBudgetDec;

                                  TotCostDec := CostControlManagement.TotCostCostObj("Control Project/Cost Object", FALSE);

                                  CostControlManagement.AllowedAndPurchCostObj(
                                    "Control Project/Cost Object", AllowedDec, AllowedHoursDec, PrevAllowedDec,
                                    PrevAllowedHoursDec, PurchaseDec, PurchResultDec, PurchCostDec,
                                    ActualPurchResultDec, TotPurchResultDec, TRUE);

                                  MatchedToOrdersDec := PurchaseDec - "Open (Purchase)";

                                  PurchResultDec := PurchResultDec - ("Risc Coverage" - "Risc Coverage Withdraw");

                                  PrognEndResultDec := CostControlManagement.PrognEndResultCostObj("Control Project/Cost Object", FALSE);

                                  SETFILTER("Purchase Action Filter", '%1', '');
                                  ActualNotOnPurchaseActionDec := CostControlManagement.TotCostCostObj("Control Project/Cost Object", TRUE);

                                  RemainingAmntDec := TotalBudgetDec - PurchBudgetDec - ActualNotOnPurchaseActionDec;

                                  Job.COPYFILTER(PrevPrognosisFilter, "Prognosis Filter");
                                  CALCFIELDS(Prognosis);
                                  PrevPrognDec := Prognosis;
                                  IF PrevPrognDec <> 0 THEN
                                    PrognDifferenceDec := PrognosisDec - PrevPrognDec
                                  ELSE
                                    PrognDifferenceDec := 0;

                                  IF ProjectCostObject.GET("Project No.", "Cost Object") THEN
                                    Description := ProjectCostObject.Name;
                                END;

               DataItemLinkReference=Job;
               DataItemLink=Project No.=FIELD(No.) }

    { 1100525100;3;Column;CostType_ControlProjectCostObject;

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportFilter@1100525000() : Text;
    BEGIN
      IF Job.GETFILTERS <> '' THEN
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2', Job.TABLECAPTION, Job.GETFILTERS));
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcProject@1100485000();
    VAR
      ExtensionContract@1100485000 : Record 11012004;
      Option@1100485003 : Record 11012502;
      JobLedgerEntry@1100485004 : Record 11072005;
      ProjectInstallment@1100485005 : Record 11012018;
      CustLedgerEntry@1100485006 : Record 21;
      VendorLedgerEntry@1100485008 : Record 25;
      PercDec@1100485007 : Decimal;
      PaidAmnt@1100485001 : Decimal;
      PaidPerc@1100485011 : Decimal;
      ControlProjectCostType@1100485012 : Record 11012046;
      MainProjFilter@1100485014 : Text[30];
      ProjFilter@1100485013 : Text[30];
    BEGIN
      ExtensionToInvoice := 0;
      ExtensionApproved := 0;
      OptionApproved := 0;
      OptionToInvoice := 0;
      ExtensionsInvoiced := 0;
      InstallmentsInvoiced := 0;
      CostPlusInvoiced := 0;
      VendorBalance := 0;
      PaidInstallments := 0;
      InstallmentsToReceive := 0;
      //ik heb het gebruik van de nieuwe variabelen ProjFilter en MainProjFilter overigens niet
      //van commentaar voorzien
      IF Job."Single/Main/Sub Project" <> Job."Single/Main/Sub Project"::"Main Project" THEN BEGIN
        MainProjFilter := '';
        ProjFilter := Job."No.";
      END ELSE BEGIN
        MainProjFilter := Job."No.";
        ProjFilter := '';
      END;
      Job.SETFILTER("Project Filter", ProjFilter);
      Job.CALCFIELDS(
        "Project Contract Amount", "Contract Amount", Budget, "Actual Costs",
        "Budget Hours (Entire Project)", "Actual Hours", "Open Hours");

      ExtensionToInvoice := 0;
      ExtensionApproved := 0;
      ExtensionContract.RESET;
      ExtensionContract.SETFILTER("Project No.", ProjFilter);
      ExtensionContract.SETFILTER("Main Project No.", MainProjFilter);
      ExtensionContract.SETFILTER("Contract Date", Job.GETFILTER("Cumulation Filter"));
      IF ExtensionContract.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          IF ExtensionContract.Status = ExtensionContract.Status::"Invoicing Allowed" THEN
            ExtensionToInvoice := ExtensionToInvoice + ExtensionContract."Contract Amount (LCY)";
          IF ExtensionContract.Status = ExtensionContract.Status::Order THEN
            ExtensionApproved :=  ExtensionApproved + ExtensionContract."Contract Amount (LCY)";
        UNTIL ExtensionContract.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      OptionToInvoice := 0;
      OptionApproved := 0;
      Option.RESET;
      Option.SETCURRENTKEY("Project No.","Plot No.",Group,"Sub Group","Contract Date");
      Option.SETFILTER("Project No.", ProjFilter);
      Option.SETFILTER("Main Project No.", MainProjFilter);
      Option.SETFILTER("Contract Date", Job.GETFILTER("Cumulation Filter"));
      Option.SETFILTER(Status, '%1..%2', Option.Status::Order, Option.Status::Invoice);
      IF Option.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          CASE Option.Status OF
            Option.Status::Order:
              OptionApproved := OptionApproved + Option."Contract Amount";
            Option.Status::Invoice:
              OptionToInvoice := OptionToInvoice + Option."Contract Amount";
          END;
        UNTIL Option.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      JobLedgerEntry.RESET;
      JobLedgerEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Job No.","Posting Date");
      JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Job No.", ProjFilter);
      JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Main Project No.", MainProjFilter);
      JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Posting Date", Job.GETFILTER("Cumulation Filter"));
      JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Entry Type", JobLedgerEntry."Entry Type"::Sale);
      JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Advance Payment", FALSE);
      JobLedgerEntry.DPA_SetFilters(CurrReport.OBJECTID(FALSE));
      IF JobLedgerEntry.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          ProjectInstallment.RESET;
          IF ProjectInstallment.GET(JobLedgerEntry."Job No.",JobLedgerEntry.Principal,
                                 JobLedgerEntry."Plot No.",JobLedgerEntry."Installment No.") THEN BEGIN
            IF (ProjectInstallment."Extension Contract" <> '') OR (ProjectInstallment.Option <> '') THEN
              ExtensionsInvoiced := ExtensionsInvoiced - JobLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)"
            ELSE
              InstallmentsInvoiced := InstallmentsInvoiced - JobLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)";
          END ELSE
            CostPlusInvoiced -= JobLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)"
        UNTIL JobLedgerEntry.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      IF (Job."Starting Date" <> 0D) AND (Job."Ending Date" <> 0D) THEN BEGIN
        ProjectDays := Job."Ending Date" - Job."Starting Date";
        CumDays := Job."Ending Date" - Job.GETRANGEMAX("Period Filter");
        IF ProjectDays <> 0 THEN
          PercTime := 100 - (CumDays / ProjectDays * 100) ;
      END;

      IF Job.Budget <> 0 THEN
        CostPerc := 100 * Job."Actual Costs" / Job.Budget
      ELSE
        CostPerc := 0;

      IF Job."Budget Hours (Entire Project)" <> 0  THEN
        LaborPerc := (Job."Actual Hours" + Job."Open Hours") / Job."Budget Hours (Entire Project)" * 100
      ELSE
        LaborPerc := 0;

      IF (Job."Contract Amount" + ExtensionToInvoice + ExtensionApproved + OptionToInvoice + OptionApproved) = 0 THEN
        PercTurnOver := 0
      ELSE
        PercTurnOver := ((InstallmentsInvoiced + ExtensionsInvoiced) /
                        (Job."Contract Amount" + ExtensionToInvoice + ExtensionApproved + OptionToInvoice + OptionApproved)) * 100;

      VendorBalance := 0;
      JobLedgerEntry.RESET;
      JobLedgerEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Job No.","Document No.","Posting Date");
      JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Job No.", ProjFilter);
      JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Main Project No.", MainProjFilter);
      JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Entry Type", JobLedgerEntry."Entry Type"::Usage);
      JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE(Surcharge, FALSE);
      JobLedgerEntry.DPA_SetFilters(CurrReport.OBJECTID(FALSE));
      IF JobLedgerEntry.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          VendorLedgerEntry.RESET;
          VendorLedgerEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Document No.");
          VendorLedgerEntry.SETFILTER(
            "Document Type", '%1|%2', VendorLedgerEntry."Document Type"::Invoice, VendorLedgerEntry."Document Type"::"Credit Memo");
          VendorLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Document No.", JobLedgerEntry."Document No.");
          VendorLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Posting Date", '..%1', Job.GETRANGEMAX("Period Filter"));
          IF VendorLedgerEntry.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
            REPEAT
              VendorLedgerEntry.CALCFIELDS("Original Amt. (LCY)", "Remaining Amt. (LCY)");
              PaidAmnt := VendorLedgerEntry."Original Amt. (LCY)" - VendorLedgerEntry."Remaining Amt. (LCY)";
              IF VendorLedgerEntry."Original Amt. (LCY)" <> 0 THEN
                PaidPerc := (PaidAmnt / VendorLedgerEntry."Original Amt. (LCY)") * 100
              ELSE
                PaidPerc := 0;
              VendorBalance := VendorBalance + (JobLedgerEntry."Total Cost (LCY)" / 100) * PaidPerc;
            UNTIL VendorLedgerEntry.NEXT = 0;
          END;
        UNTIL JobLedgerEntry.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      PaidInstallments := 0;
      InstallmentsToReceive := 0;
      PaidCostPlus := 0;
      CostPlusToReceive := 0;
      JobLedgerEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Project Invoice", "Installment Invoice", "Job No.", Principal, "Installment No.");
      JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Project Invoice", TRUE);
      //JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Installment Invoice", TRUE);
      JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Job No.", ProjFilter);
      JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Main Project No.", MainProjFilter);
      JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Entry Type", JobLedgerEntry."Entry Type"::Sale);
      JobLedgerEntry.SETFILTER("Posting Date", Job.GETFILTER("Cumulation Filter"));
      JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Advance Payment", FALSE);
      JobLedgerEntry.DPA_SetFilters(CurrReport.OBJECTID(FALSE));
      IF JobLedgerEntry.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          CustLedgerEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Document No.");
          CustLedgerEntry.SETFILTER(
            "Document Type", '%1|%2', CustLedgerEntry."Document Type"::Invoice, CustLedgerEntry."Document Type"::"Credit Memo");
          CustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Document No.", JobLedgerEntry."Document No.");
          IF CustLedgerEntry.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
            CustLedgerEntry.CALCFIELDS("Amount (LCY)","Remaining Amt. (LCY)");
            IF CustLedgerEntry."Amount (LCY)" <> 0 THEN BEGIN
              PercDec := (-1 * JobLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)") / CustLedgerEntry."Amount (LCY)";
              IF JobLedgerEntry."Installment Invoice" THEN
                PaidInstallments := PaidInstallments + (PercDec * (CustLedgerEntry."Amount (LCY)" - CustLedgerEntry."Remaining Amt. (LCY)"))
              ELSE
                PaidCostPlus := PaidCostPlus + (PercDec * (CustLedgerEntry."Amount (LCY)" - CustLedgerEntry."Remaining Amt. (LCY)"))
            END;
          END;
          IF JobLedgerEntry."Installment Invoice" THEN
            InstallmentsToReceive := InstallmentsToReceive + (JobLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)" * -1)
          ELSE
            CostPlusToReceive := CostPlusToReceive + (JobLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)" * -1);
        UNTIL JobLedgerEntry.NEXT = 0;

      InstallmentsToReceive := InstallmentsToReceive - PaidInstallments;
      CostPlusToReceive := CostPlusToReceive - PaidCostPlus;

      IF NOT ControlProjectCostType.GET(Job."No.", ControlProjectCostType."Cost Type"::Labor) THEN BEGIN
         ControlProjectCostType.INIT;
         ControlProjectCostType."Project No." := Job."No.";
         ControlProjectCostType."Main Project No." := Job."Main Project";
         ControlProjectCostType."Cost Type" := ControlProjectCostType."Cost Type"::Labor;
      END;
      Job.COPYFILTER("Cumulation Filter", ControlProjectCostType."Cumulation Filter");
      Job.COPYFILTER("Project Filter", ControlProjectCostType."Project Filter");
      ControlProjectCostType.CALCFIELDS("Actual Costs");
      LaborCost := ControlProjectCostType."Actual Costs";

      Prognosis.RESET;
      Prognosis.SETRANGE("Project No.", Job."No.");
      Prognosis.SETRANGE("Prognosis Date", Job."Prognosis Filter");
      IF NOT Prognosis.FINDFIRST THEN
        Prognosis.INIT;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
